t.Cfg.IndexGateway.Mode\n846: \tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.IndexGatewayClientConfig.Mode = t.Cfg.IndexGateway.Mode\n847: \n848: \tif t.Cfg.IndexGateway.Mode == indexgateway.RingMode {\n849: 200,\n870: \t\t\t\t// This is a small hack to save some CPU cycles.\n871: \t\t\t\t// We check if the object is still valid after pulling it from cache using the IndexCacheValidity value\n872: \t\t\t\t// however it has to be deserialized to do so, setting the cache validity to some arbitrary amount less than the\n873: \t\t\t\t// IndexCacheValidity guarantees the Embedded cache will expire the object first which can be done without\n874: \t\t\t\t// having to deserialize the object.\n875: \t\t\t\tTTL: t.Cfg.StorageConfig.IndexCacheValidity - 1*time.Minute,\n876: \t\t\t},\n877: \n886: \tcase t.Cfg.isTarget(Querier), t.Cfg.isTarget(Ruler), t.Cfg.isTarget(Read), t.Cfg.isTarget(Backend), t.isModuleActive(IndexGateway), t.Cfg.isTarget(BloomPlanner), server.\n1908: \t\tfor _, s := range servicesToWaitFor() {\n1909: \t\t\t_ = s.AwaitTerminated(context.Background())\n1910: \t\t}\n1911: \n1912: \t\t// shutdown HTTP and gRPC servers (this also It also scales better.\n6: \n7: The router is optimized for high performance and a small memory footprint. It scales well even with very long paths and a large number of routes. \\tc.Server.MetricsNamespace = constants.Loki\\n135: \\tc.Server.ExcludeRequestInLog = true\\n136: \\n137: \\t// Set the default module list to 'all'\\n138: \\tc.Target = []string{All}\\n139: \\tf.Var(&c.Target, \\\"target\\\",\\n140: \\t\\t\\\"A comma-separated list of components to run. \\\"+\\n141: \\t\\t\\t\\\"The default value 'all' runs Loki in single binary mode. \\\"+\\n142: \\t\\t\\t\\\"The value 'read' is an alias to run only read-path related components such as the querier and query-frontend, but all in the same process. \\\"+\\n143: \\t\\t\\t\\\"The value 'write' is an alias to run only write-path related components such as the distributor and compactor, but all in the same process. \\\"+\\n144: \\t\\t\\t\\\"Supported values: all, compactor, distributor, ingester, querier, query-scheduler, ingester-querier, query-frontend, index-gateway, ruler, table-manager, read, write. \\\"+\\n145: \\t\\t\\t\\\"A full list of available targets can be printed when running Loki with the '-list-targets' command line flag. \\\",\\n146: \\t)\\n147: \\tf.BoolVar(&c.AuthEnabled, \\\"auth.enabled\\\", true,\\n148: \\t\\t\\\"Enables authentication through the X-Scope-OrgID header, which must be present if true. \\\"+\\n149: \\t\\t\\t\\\"If false, the OrgID will always be set to 'fake'.\\\",\\n150: \\t)\\n151: \\tf.IntVar(&c.BallastBytes, \\\"config.ballast-bytes\\\", 0,\\n152: \\t\\t\\\"The amount of virtual memory in bytes to reserve as ballast in order to optimize garbage collection. \\\"+\\n153: \\t\\t\\t\\\"Larger ballasts result in fewer garbage collection passes, reducing CPU overhead at the cost of heap size. \\\"+\\n154: \\t\\t\\t\\\"The ballast will not consume physical memory, because it is never read from. \\\"+\\n155: \\t\\t\\t\\\"It will, however, distort metrics, because it is counted as live memory. \\\",\\n156: \\t)\\n157: \\n158: \\tf.BoolVar(&c.LegacyReadTarget, \\\"legacy-read-mode\\\", false,
